Tianjin Airplane Arrives in Jinan from Peiping 82

The Aviation Company establishes a resident office in Jinan. Jinan Correspondence: The "Tianjin" airplane, which was test-flown from Peiping to Jinan, passed through Jinan to Tianjin and back to Peiping a few days ago. Today (12th) at 10:30 AM, the original airplane was flown directly from the north by Nie Kaiyi, Deputy Director of the Air Navigation Group, and four others. It landed at the Zhangzhuang Airport in Jinan. Nie and others stayed at the Jinan Hotel. Nie told reporters that he flew out of Peiping at 8:30 AM today. After entering Shandong Province, the sky was filled with yellow dust. After flying in the sky for about ten minutes after arriving in Jinan, he saw the airport and landed. Wang Zhenxiang, a radio engineer who was traveling with him, stayed in Peiping. This time, the pilots Zhang Huayi, the mechanics Yu Yongquan and Yu Shiping, and four brothers came. The results of this test flight were excellent. The Peiping-Jinan route will be officially opened on the first of next month. Two airplanes will be used in the future. One will fly north from the capital and the other will fly south from Peiping at 8:01 AM every day, and they can arrive at 3 or 4 PM. There will be three stops along the way: Xuzhou, Jinan, and Tianjin. Jinan has decided to set up a resident office of the Aviation Company in Jinan, and Zhu Fengzao, the station chief of the Air Navigation Department of the Ministry of Military Affairs in Jinan, and a Mr. Gu have been requested to handle the office. The office is located in the YMCA. It is reported that Nie and his party are scheduled to return to Beijing tomorrow (12th).

Qingdao Municipal Government Reorganizes Municipal Property 83

Qingdao Correspondence: Since the receipt of the land and real estate owned by the city of Qingdao, the Qingdao Municipal Government has followed the old rules of previous administrations without reorganizing it. As a result, there are many malpractices and citizens have complained. Now, in order to be cautious about the city's property and increase revenue, a reorganization plan has been drafted and submitted to the 81st Municipal Meeting for discussion and decision. The content is divided into two items: land and housing, which are roughly as follows:

(1) Land: In the past, the land rented out by the city was not made public. Secrecy breeds malpractices, and it is necessary to thoroughly publicize it to eliminate malpractices. The Finance Bureau has been ordered to draft rules for bidding for open land. The area and grade of the rented land will be announced in advance, and then citizens will bid for it. Public bidding will be used, and the highest bidder will be the tenant, eliminating the previous malpractices.

(2) Real Estate: In addition to the real estate sold by the Municipal Bureau during the German era, the city has more than 260 properties. Since the German operation, it has not been reorganized. The city government has decided on two methods: A. For those that should be repaired and rebuilt, three methods are formulated: 1. Those that are dilapidated and need to be repaired will be surveyed and estimated by the Finance Bureau, and the Municipal Government will allocate funds for repairs at any time. 2. Those that have collapsed and cannot be repaired and have no need for rebuilding will be estimated at a price and allowed to be purchased by citizens. The land will still be handled in accordance with the regulations for publicly rented land in the city. 3. For the city's property in prosperous areas, the original buildings should be rebuilt in order to revitalize the market and increase revenue, or citizens may undertake the construction and be responsible for the renovation. The property rights still belong to the city (the undertaking method will be stipulated separately). As for where repairs should be made, where sales can be made, and where renovations can be made by citizens themselves, the Finance Bureau will investigate and report to the Municipal Government for approval. B. For those that should be re-priced, the rent for the city's real estate was evaluated in 1924. Many years have passed and it should be re-evaluated. Now, all the city's property has been divided into areas, re-numbered, and maps have been drawn for easy investigation. At the same time, the price will be verified and the rent will be determined to increase revenue. Central agencies, local organizations, and other agencies that borrow it should also pay rent to show uniformity. For those used by the Japanese at that time, the rent was used to offset interest due to loan relations, and it should also be listed as income and expenditure for future reference. Other real estate along the Jiaoji Railway will be discussed with the Jiaoji Railway Bureau to exchange the city's houses with the bureau's houses for easy management. After the Finance Bureau drafts specific plans for the above two methods, they will be implemented step by step. (March 11th)

Recent Situation in Western Sichuan 84

The Ministry of Military Affairs received a report from Beijing. News from western Sichuan, being a remote border region, is quite scarce. Recently, the Ministry of Military Affairs received a report from the area detailing the social and commercial situation. The following is extracted for the reference of those concerned about western Sichuan:

(1) Administrative Scope: The Han army controls ten border counties in Sichuan and Gansu. The total area, with Songpan as the headquarters (Sichuan border), extends west to the Qinghai border and the Tibetan borders of Maogong, Lifan, Wenchuan, Weizhou, Maoxian, etc. (Gansu border) The area bordering Sichuan and Gansu includes Wenxian, Xigu, Taozhou, Minzhou, Daohe, etc., totaling ten counties.

(2) Regional Situation: The area currently held by the Han army is the center of the four provinces of Sichuan, Gansu, Qinghai, and Tibet.

(3) Ethnic Groups: There are several types of Yi people. Due to the vastness of the border area, these people mostly live a scattered existence, with no fixed abode, dwelling in rock and forest. Furthermore, communication is obstructed, and culture is not easily introduced, leading to language barriers and making accurate surveys difficult.

(4) Industry Status: Zhangla in Songpan is a famous gold mountain, but unfortunately, primitive mining methods are used. It produces approximately 10,000 to 20,000 taels of gold annually. If machinery and new methods were used, the amount of gold mined would certainly increase many times over. Other resources, such as the copper mine on Gongkang Ridge, the iron mine at Fengdong Pass, and the coal mine at Sanshe, are all natural riches but are unexploited. Furthermore, the gold mines at Erkai, Songping, Manseergu, and the silver mine at Bipenggou are all closed due to the local Tibetan people's superstitious beliefs in Feng Shui, which is a great pity.

(5) Commercial Status: Because of the cold weather and barren land in the counties under its jurisdiction, agriculture is not very developed. Fortunately, Han and Tibetan people live together and trade with each other. Consequently, foreign merchants come here to trade in droves, especially from Shaanxi and Henan. Mutual trust is evident, and commerce is quite developed.

(6) People's Beliefs: The people of each county are Han, Hui, and Tibetan. Because of their different ethnicities, they have different beliefs. For example, mosques are built everywhere for Muslims to worship. Both Han and Tibetan people believe in Buddhism, especially the Tibetans, who are the most devout. There are large-scale Buddhist temples everywhere. Every three years, the living Buddhas from various places go to Tibet to pay homage to the Dalai Lama and the Panchen Lama. When the Dalai Lama rebelled against China, he sent representatives to incite the Tibetan people to surrender to the British. Fortunately, in the 18th year of the Republic, Commander Yang arrived outside the pass at Damoa and convened a meeting of officials from various Tibetan tribes, explaining the greater meaning of the central government, instructing them to lean towards the central government and not surrender to British imperialism. All the officials respectfully obeyed. As for the Bo people (commonly called Bo Guozi), they are even more fierce than the Tibetans, delighting in robbery and killing.

(7) Customs and Habits: The customs and habits of the Tibetan people are very different from those of the Han people. Some tribal chiefs have held their positions since the Han and Tang dynasties. The local autonomous organization functions as follows: when an event occurs, the chiefs convene a meeting of the Tibetan people. First, a shaman speaks, expressing opinions, which are then voted on. Then, the strong men's meeting votes again. Finally, the elders' meeting makes the final decision, and then the chief executes it. Marriages often involve cattle and sheep as gifts. Funerals mostly use cremation. Muslim weddings do not involve welcoming the bride to the ancestral hall, and funerals do not use coffins, but rather the corpse is wrapped in cloth and carried for burial. Han people's coming-of-age, weddings, and funerals are the same as in other provinces. Bo people's marriages mostly result from robbery, and funerals also use cremation. (Daily News)

Details of the Verdict in the Ye Yixiong Case 85

Shenyang Correspondence: The case of Ye Yixiong, a candidate magistrate of the Special District Local Court, involving attempted murder and embezzlement, was publicly tried twice in the Criminal Court of the Shenyang Local Court. After the last debate concluded, the official verdict was pronounced on the 9th, sentencing the defendant to life imprisonment and depriving him of his civil rights for life. A brief report has already been published previously. The following details the circumstances of the verdict in the case:

The case, involving a judicial official as the perpetrator, had already attracted the attention of the legal community. The transfer of the case to Shenyang's jurisdiction further increased its gravity. Therefore, before the verdict was reached, the presiding judge of the Criminal Court, Tang Yinfen, along with judges Yang Yangcheng and Li Hongwen, held a deliberation to jointly discuss opinions and carefully examine the defendant's confessions. The verdict was then submitted to the president of the court, Zhang Qihong, for review. The procedures for pronouncing the verdict were then completed. On the morning of the 9th, at 11:00 AM, the defendant Ye Yixiong was brought from the detention center to the court's waiting room. At 2:10 PM, the presiding judge Tang Yinfen, along with judges Yang Yangcheng and Li Hongwen, and official Jian Hongjun, clerk Wang Chan'gui, all arrived in court. The court police removed Ye's shackles and brought him to the First Civil Court to hear the verdict. Wang Ce'an, the lawyer defending Ye, also appeared in court. The case file was first handed to Ye to allow him to review the testimony for any errors before signing. During the hearing of the verdict, Ye's face changed, as if he were frightened. The audience in the gallery also sat upright, holding their breath and waiting. However, during this period, Ye nitpicked his previous statements, such as "October 5th is the death anniversary of her deceased husband." The original record of the fifth day was perhaps a mistake. There were also errors in other answers. The clerk corrected them one by one. After reading and signing, the presiding judge announced the official verdict. The presiding judge, the judges, the prosecutor, and the defense counsel all stood up. The presiding judge then held the verdict and read the main text, saying, "In the case of the defendant Ye Yixiong for attempted murder and embezzlement, the verdict is as follows: The defendant Ye Yixiong is sentenced to life imprisonment for attempted murder and embezzlement, and is deprived of his civil rights for life. For possessing military firearms and ammunition, he is sentenced to one year of imprisonment. The life sentence and deprivation of civil rights are to be executed." During the second public trial, Ye had requested the presiding judge not to impose or reduce the portion of the sentence that deprived him of his civil rights, because he had already anticipated that no matter how severe the crime he committed, there would come a day when he would be released and see the light of day again. At that time, the expiration of the deprivation of civil rights would allow him to practice law again. Unexpectedly, both the prison sentence and the deprivation of rights were for life. Upon hearing this, he could not help but take a deep breath of cold air. At the time, Presiding Judge Tang feared that he might not understand the main text clearly and explained it to him, saying that the other crimes had already been sentenced to life imprisonment, and that the possession of military firearms and ammunition could not be executed. Ye asked again on what grounds. The presiding judge said there were two reasons: (1) The defendant traveled by train from Harbin to Ping, and the journey was very safe. There was no need to carry a gun. The fact that he carried a gun without needing to, and that he did not have a gun license, or even knew the number of his old gun license, clearly showed that he had a premeditated plan to murder. (2) According to the defendant's confession, it was powerful evidence of premeditated murder. As the defendant confessed, "On the train, I saw a love letter in the suitcase that she had not sent to Liu Kelong. In it, there was 'The Mid-Autumn Festival is coming, have this mooncake,' etc. After reading it, I would kill her." The defendant, after seeing the letter on the train, did not shoot Zhang Liqing, but tricked her off the train and walked a long way, shooting her in a remote place. The time for consideration was enough to constitute premeditated murder. In addition, ordinary people are not allowed to carry guns and must have a gun license. The defendant carried a gun without a license, so according to the regulations on carrying military firearms and ammunition, he should be found guilty. Ye asked again whether embezzlement was also a crime. The presiding judge said that embezzlement was also established, but according to Article 74 of the Criminal Law, embezzlement was intentionally punished more severely, and he was not simply sentenced to imprisonment, but rather the crimes were combined. The presiding judge added that the defendant was sentenced to life imprisonment because the murder was only attempted, so the sentence was reduced by one-third. The verdict would be delivered to the defendant in the future. If the defendant did not agree, he could appeal to the High Court within ten days. At that time, Ye, upon hearing the verdict of life imprisonment, suddenly seemed dazed. He asked the presiding judge when the appeal should be made. The presiding judge said that the appeal could be filed after the verdict was delivered. Ye asked again whether he could appeal immediately. The presiding judge said that according to procedural law, the defendant could not appeal until he submitted a statement of appeal. At this point, Ye pondered for a long time without speaking. The presiding judge then announced the adjournment. Ye's face was pale, and he lowered his head and retreated. It is heard that Ye has decided to submit an appeal to the High Court within the deadline. (March 11)

Lecture on the Mission of the Kuomintang 86

(Continued)

Some people think that revolution does not need any party. As long as farmers, workers, merchants, and students unite and, so-called, rise up and fight, the revolutionary cause can succeed. I dare say that this kind of thinking is already outdated. Historically, there have been such revolutionary movements, but how many have succeeded? It could not succeed in the era of rural economy or handicraft economy. Can it be realized in the modern society of the scientific world? The failure of the Boxer Rebellion thirty years ago is a clear example. We believe that all revolutionary undertakings must first have an ideology that meets the needs of the times, unite people who believe in the same ideology, and organize a strict party before the revolution can succeed. Otherwise, a pile of loose sand is bound to fail. Just look at the map after the European war. Those that were formerly destroyed are now restored, and those that were formerly weak are now strong, such as Poland and Turkey, are all because they have parties. As for the Fascist Party of Italy and the Communist Party of Soviet Russia, they have succeeded today because they first had a strong party to lead the revolution and construction.

However, the Chinese Kuomintang is also different from the Italian Fascist Party and the Russian Communist Party. They advocate one-party dictatorship, while the Chinese Kuomintang only advocates using the party to govern until the constitutional period, when it will hand over power to the people of the whole country and the elected government. This is clearly stipulated in the Founding Program personally drafted by the Premier. However, just after the obstacles to nation-building have been removed, the people's political awareness and ability to exercise their four rights of election, recall, initiative, and referendum are not yet developed. On the one hand, the Party should take advantage of the historical mission of the Party to guide the people to exercise their political power. At the same time, it should represent the people and exercise their political power to suppress reactionaries and complete the responsibility of tutelage.

The Northeast is bordered by two major red and white imperialist powers, Soviet Russia in the north and Japan in the south. They encroach on the hinterland with political and economic power, which is tantamount to joint management, or what the Premier called a sub-colony. I said last year that to save China, we must first save the Northeast. To save the Northeast, Russia and Japan must completely abandon their so-called special interests in the Northeast, because as long as there is any imperialist power within the country, no matter where, it cannot be considered an independent and equal country. This is only in terms of diplomacy. If we use the power of the Chinese national economy to purchase it, we will feel even more discouraged. In European and American industrialized countries, the difficulty they feel is only the problem of uneven distribution, while in our country, it is the problem of production, because our production mechanisms are very corrupt, and our production capacity is very weak. All the organizations of production have not yet escaped the state of the European Middle Ages. Most of the daily necessities of the people depend on foreign countries. The most ridiculous thing is that China, which has been called an agricultural country for thousands of years, is now continuously importing Japanese rice and American wheat. As for the materials used for other clothes and houses, everything seen in the cities is foreign goods, not to mention steel and electricity. Foreigners have a saying to protect sales in China, saying, "China's consumption is the newest and largest in the world, and China's production is the oldest and lowest in the world." Can we deny that to develop the national economy, we must first develop the Northeast and Northwest? The Premier also solemnly said in the Founding Strategy that I believe that from the perspective of transportation and diplomacy, developing the Northeast is more convenient and urgent.

In short, if we want China to be independent and equal, and we want the problem of the Chinese national economy to be fully resolved, we should gather the minds and financial resources of the people of the whole country to first develop the Northeast. Soon, the Party headquarters in the four eastern provinces will be established. I hope that the comrades and compatriots in the Northeast will all walk under the banner of the Blue Sky, White Sun, towards the bright road of the Three Principles of the People, and jointly complete the mission of saving the country and building the nation. (End)

Zhejiang Province Maintains Construction Funding 87

Construction funds must not be diverted without approval, and construction donations will continue to be collected as before. The Zhejiang Construction Department recently investigated the construction funds of various counties in Zhejiang Province and found that they were often diverted for other purposes without authorization. These diversions were nominally temporary loans but were actually entangled with other matters, with no definite repayment date. This made it impossible to determine the amount of funding available, and when matters needed to be handled, there were no funds to draw upon. This not only hampered construction but also disrupted public finances. It was therefore necessary to rectify and reorganize this situation. The Department therefore issued a joint order with the Finance Department to all counties yesterday, stating that all construction funds in each county, except for the budgeted expenditures, could not be diverted for other purposes without special approval. Those who had already diverted funds without authorization were given one month from the date of the order to repay the full amount. The counties whose funds had been handed over to the Financial Affairs Bureau for management were immediately ordered to instruct the county magistrates to work with the bureau chiefs to clear up the accounts within the prescribed time limit and ensure that the funds were kept in a special account without any shortage. Otherwise, they would be severely punished.

The Department also stated that since the implementation of the tax reduction in Zhejiang Province, all taxes similar to transit duties had been abolished by order. The impact of this had led to the suspension of construction donations that were previously collected independently by local authorities. Recently, the county magistrates had successively submitted requests for instructions on how to provide relief. After investigating this matter, it was found that these construction donations had been in place for many years, based on local real estate or goods as the standard, collected through local government agencies by entrusted merchants, and were completely different from transit duties collected by bureaus. Since they were neither within the scope of transit duties nor similar to them, their nature should be clarified and maintained so that local construction projects could be maintained in a normal state. A proposal was drafted and submitted to the 382nd meeting of the provincial government, which passed a resolution that all donations collected by various counties for construction purposes in the past would be allowed to continue to be collected as before. The provincial government issued an order to all counties yesterday to inform them of this decision.

Zhang Zhijiang Inspects Pacification Troops 88

Jiangsu Pacification Commissioner Zhang Zhijiang this morning (the 14th) took a special Fengyun company's special boat Fengyun small boat and tugboat Fuqing to inspect pacification work in the Jiangbei area and inspect the pacification troops. Those who departed with Zhang included Chief of Staff Yu Dianshu, Chief Secretary Sun Zhicheng, Chief Adjutant Wang Ruchun, Councilor Song Bangjie, Councilor Wang Ziping, Staff Officer Zhu Chang, Staff Officer Zhang Jingyuan, Secretary Song Zhenhua, Gao Lixun, Quartermaster Liu XiHui, Adjutants Guo Lanting, Dong Wenfu, Li Chengbin, Li Yuanzhi, Gao Ruwei, Ge Zuzhou, Liu Shengkun, Li Baozhen, Zang Yuqi, Yu Gfei, Wang Zhaocheng, Lu Baozhen, and the pistol team guard team, totaling about one hundred and dozens of people. It is heard that Zhang's trip is scheduled for the first day to Qingjiang, the second day to inspect the pistol special artillery three independent regiments stationed in Qingjiang, the third day to inspect the 96th Brigade and the 5th Independent Brigade stationed in Huaian Yangzhuang, the fourth day to inspect the 95th Brigade stationed in Suqian, the fifth day to inspect the 3rd Cavalry Division stationed in Suining, the sixth day to inspect the 1st Cavalry Division stationed in Yaowan, and the seventh day, he will take the Longhai Jinpu train from Yaowan to Yunhe Station to transfer to the Beijing-Shanghai train and return to Yang, at that time, he may detour to the capital to visit Chairman Jiang and present important official matters.

The Zhejiang Provincial Pawnshop Association believes that according to the regulations, pawnshops that have been looted by bandits do not need to compensate, and has telegraphed to the provincial government to order the county to make an announcement. Local Correspondence

Songjiang 90

The Steamed Bone Examination in the Hu Murder Case: The Hu family of Dawuqiao, Songjiang, was originally a prominent family in the county seat. Unfortunately, the Hu Yinglong murder case occurred last year. Zhang Zeyu, the brother of the wife, and others reported to the County Court Procuratorate that Hu Yinglong and his aunt Hu Nie smothered his sister to death and requested that justice be served. The defendant was arrested and went to the place where the coffin was placed and opened the coffin for inspection. The local coroner verified that there were finger marks on the neck, proving that she had been smothered to death, but the Western doctor hired by the informant believed that the death spots had contradictory opinions. The case was repeatedly tried, and a public prosecution was filed for the crime of premeditated murder. The defendant Hu Yinglong hired lawyer Zhang Baopei to defend him, and Gu Shouyi, a lawyer appointed by the court, defended Hu Nie pro bono. There was once a public trial, and the defendant's lawyer had many doubts about the contradiction between the coroner and the doctor's appraisal and requested a review to clarify the truth. The court approved, but the death had been several months, and the body should have rotted. It was necessary to conduct a steamed bone review. A verification site was set up at Longmen Temple in the South Gate, and various utensils for the steamed verification were prepared. Zhenjiang coroner Guo Chunrong was appointed to take charge. It was very secretive beforehand. Until yesterday, both parties were notified to conduct the review this morning (the 14th). Guo Li arrived in Songjiang yesterday. This morning at 8 o'clock, Prosecutor Li, Judge Li, Clerk Guo, Coroner Tao, and others arrived at the venue first. The defendants Hu Yinglong and Hu Nie, and lawyer Gu Shouyi, and the informant Zhang Zeyu all went to report. Li Judge took the seat and announced the review. He immediately ordered Zhang Zeyu, Hu Yinglong, and Hu Nie to make a bond to prove that the coffin was indeed Hu Zhang's. Guo Li first ordered the soil to open the coffin and take out the dead body on the mat and wash it. By 4 pm, it had not yet been steamed for verification, so whether there were injuries was not visible and had to wait until the steam verification was continued tomorrow before a decision could be made. The bones at the verification site were temporarily sealed and ordered police to guard the law. The judge and coroner returned to the hospital, and the two defendants were still returned to custody.

Suzhou 91

A Large Batch of Reactionary Criminals Escorted to Suzhou: Rugaoxian yesterday (14th) again ordered police to escort the anti-revolutionary criminal Wang Wenfu, Shen Jiuhou, Zhang Zhushan, Deng Wuzong, Bao Hua, Shen Mingjun, Zhang Changlin, Chen Yuerui, Ma Longer, Sun Yulin, Zhu Guilin, Sha Zhonggui, Shi Youwen, Huang Yincai, Tao Wanfu, Ma Dagen, Zhang Erzhang, Wu Rongqing, Wu Youquan, Zhu Changqing, Hu Zhibao, Zhou Yongmin, Huang Zhengbang, and other twenty-three people to Suzhou for delivery to the High Court. After investigation by the procuratorate, they were sent to the Third Branch Prison. The Provincial Pawnshop Industry Convenes a Meeting in Suzhou: Previously, the Pawnshop Associations of various counties in Jiangsu Province had difficulty implementing the new regulations on overdue redemption interest. They had repeatedly convened meetings and sent representatives to the province to petition. The provincial government and the Construction Department had approved the temporary suspension of the new regulations and allowed the provincial pawnshop industry to continue to convene meetings to discuss a proper solution before determining the date of implementation. It was decided to convene a meeting in Suzhou on March 15. Representatives of the Pawnshop Associations of Nanjing, Wuxi, Wujin, Yixing, Liyang, Changshu, Jiangyin, Danyang, and other counties, as well as representatives of the Shanghai Office of the Provincial Association, arrived in Suzhou yesterday afternoon. A preparatory meeting was held on the same day, and Zhou Guren was elected chairman to discuss the reorganization of the Provincial Association. Of the county trade associations, ten have been reorganized and established, and seven are in the process of being reorganized. According to the regulations, a provincial association can be organized with more than one-fifth of the members. Therefore, the association urgently needs to prepare for reorganization and first set up an office in Zhenjiang. In addition to urging the seven counties that are in the process of being reorganized to speed up their establishment, the ten counties that have been established should send the list of committee members and the charter to Zhenjiang for the preparation of the Provincial Association office. The speaker then reported that the two cases of self-posting by the current household and the shortening of the time limit are most closely related to the interests of the pawn industry itself, and the department will wait for the resolution at the general meeting. Also, the Wuxian Pawnshop Trade Association proposed to suggest that the time limit for the redemption of gold be shortened to alleviate the impact of the high price of gold.

Gao Ying's Wife's Illness Worsens in Prison: Liao, the wife of Gao Ying, who is detained at the Sifen Prison on Siqian Street, has been ill. Li Guangxun and Gu Yuecha of Boxue Hospital have been repeatedly asked to diagnose and treat her, and they believe that the environment is unsuitable and it is difficult to recover. It is now learned that since this year, she has been coughing up blood, coughing, losing her eyes, lying in bed, and her shape has disappeared. Ding, the prison director, intends to transfer her to the hospital for treatment under the guarantee of the hospital in accordance with the prison regulations, and to send guards to the hospital to monitor her. After she recovers, she will be brought back for execution. He has ordered Gao Ying to inform his relatives to come to Suzhou to negotiate with Boxue Hospital on the guarantee issue so that she can be transferred to the hospital immediately. The Kidnapping Bandits Captured in Shanghai are Escorted to Suzhou: Li Weibo, Sun Xiaodi, Chen Yongfa, Zhang Along, Zhang Agen, and other five members of the kidnapping gang in Weiting who were captured at the Luming Hotel in Shanghai yesterday (14th) were escorted back to Suzhou by Zhou Hongjiang, the leader of the detective team.

Wuxi 92

The Report of a Smoke Search Causing a Disturbance and a False Report of Robbery: Zhang Ada, a villager from Banqiao Town, the 8th District (Huai Xia City), came to the city the day before yesterday to report to the County Public Security Bureau that Xu Shengwu (the son of the deceased Xu Meibo), a wealthy man in Banqiao, was secretly smoking opium at home. Upon receiving the report, Director Xu immediately dispatched Detective Team Leader Zai Shouquan to lead seven or eight detectives to search the countryside. The reporter Zhang Ada again notified Xu Shengwu that today the public security agency in the city would send people to check for smoke. Xu, upon hearing this, summoned twenty or thirty thugs to ambush inside the house on both sides of the hall. After Detective Dai and others arrived at Xu's house, they went inside to search. Unexpectedly, Xu's relief room Lu Zhongxin dared to instigate the thugs to surround Detective Dai and others, refuse the search, and even use force. Xu Shengwu went to the 1st Squad of the 2nd Platoon of the Tantangqiao Police to falsely report a robbery. Detective Dai and others, outnumbered, only brought the reporter Zhang Ada to the bureau to report. Director Xu, upon receiving the report, was furious and dispatched more police to the countryside to arrest Xu Shengwu and the relief room Lu Zhongxin to be dealt with according to law. The Eligibility Standards for People's Congress Elections are Emailed: The Wuxi County Government received an order to prepare for the election of the People's Congress and has divided the various legal groups to rush to create various rosters overnight, along with the party department's permit certificate and the certification documents approved by the county government for filing. There are a total of seventy-two groups that have been sent to the county for forwarding, including forty-eight trade unions, twenty business associations and other industry groups, and four free professional journalist and lawyer associations. Two police officers were dispatched yesterday to send the applications to the province for review. At the same time, the Election Supervisor, County Chief Pan, received an email from the provincial government regarding the standards for the qualifications of the groups participating in the election: (1) Those previously filed with the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and the Ministry of Industry; (2) Those whose regulations have been reviewed and approved by the Provincial Department of Construction; (3) Those whose establishment has been reported by the County Party Department and reviewed and found to be in compliance with the organizational laws. Those who meet one of the above conditions must be registered and sent, and it is stipulated that the deadline for industrial and commercial groups is extended to the 20th, and the deadline for farmers' groups is extended to April 3 because they have just been ordered to organize.

The Bereaved Families of the Overturned Wheel Case Schedule a Petition: The Tai Li Company's Heng Yi wheel ship sank in Nantang on the 14th of last month, resulting in the tragic death of ten people. The prosecution has filed a public prosecution with the prosecutor's office for the crime of causing death by negligence. The bereaved family, by the Joint Association of Bereaved Families, by Shao Dai, reported to the reporter the process of the case and the biographies of the deceased, and stated two points: (1) Please uphold justice and assist the bereaved families to achieve the goal of arresting and resolving the compensation for damages as soon as possible; (2) The responsibility for this case should be borne entirely by the Tai Li Company in fact. On the same day, the bereaved family continued to hold a meeting to discuss the follow-up plan and decided: (1) To Party and government agencies, we are willing to schedule another meeting on the afternoon of the 15th to discuss the petition procedures; (2) On the morning of the 16th, all the bereaved families will support the old and the young, hold flags, and go to the County Party Department, the County Government, the Construction Bureau, and other agencies to request that the property of Tai Li Company be sealed up as compensation; (3) Yang Xiangqi, the manager of Tai Li Company, serves as the captain of the Houzhai Business Group Detachment and has always relied on his power to act recklessly and oppress the villagers. He should be asked to have the business group association dismiss him from his post and give him appropriate sanctions.

Changzhou 93

Wucheng Military Police Jointly Suppress Bandits: The military and police teams of Wujin and Jiangyin counties set out jointly on the 11th of this month to search for bandits in the Wangjiao border area. On the 12th, the Wu County side captured two bandits, Huang Borong and Wang Laibao, in Xutang. Huang Borong was escorted to Jiangyin, and Wang Laibao was escorted to Wujin. In addition, the provincial guard team stationed in Tangqiao, led by Battalion Commander Shen, together with the local security group, broke into Chicken Mound on the 13th and captured the famous bandit monk Yuan Lai, who was immediately sent to the county, nailed with shackles, and imprisoned. Also, the Baoweituan of the fourth district of Xiaoxin captured three suspected bandits, Wan Genhai, Yang Fusheng, and Yang Liangsheng, and sent them to the county at the same time. However, when the military police were searching in Huangjia Lane, one person escaped on the way, and the police team opened fire and pursued, resulting in a stray bullet hitting and killing him.

A Robbery Occurred Near Mahang Bridge: At about 1:00 AM on the 13th, more than a dozen bandits suddenly came to the Chen Ziquan family's house near Tangmen, Mahang Bridge, outside the East Gate of Wu County, and broke into the house to commit robbery. The perpetrators were tied up, and they searched for clothes and jewelry, mostly silver, and 80 yuan in cash, and left.

Changshu 94

Recent News on Land Seizure Case: On the 2nd of this month, local ruffians led by Qian Linlin gathered a crowd at Dayi Bridge in this county and seized a large quantity of opium from a sand boat, hiding it privately. On the 5th, the Public Security Bureau apprehended the ringleader Qian Linlin and a large quantity of opium. They were immediately escorted to the county government and sealed for safekeeping. Qian Linlin and others were interrogated by the county government and temporarily detained pending the arrest of the remaining perpetrators. Although the county government had indicated after the incident that the case was significant and required instructions from the provincial authorities, there has been no response to date. The local Anti-Drug Society is deeply concerned about this case and held an emergency meeting on the afternoon of the 12th, resolving two matters: (1) The Anti-Drug Society should telegraph the Anti-Drug Association to request the provincial government to commend and reward the officers of the Public Security Bureau who were involved, in order to encourage them. (2) Although the seized opium has been sealed by the county government, in order to quickly eliminate the harm of drugs, the provincial government and the Civil Affairs Department of the High Court should be requested to send personnel to supervise its burning as soon as possible. Both matters have been addressed separately.

Recent Developments of the Shouzhou Branch of Zhejiang Industrial Bank: In recent years, the banking and money industries in this county have flourished, with various entities organizing banks and money shops. Recently, Zhejiang Industrial Bank and China Industrial Bank are both preparing to establish branches in Changshu. The Zhejiang Industrial Bank has repeatedly sent personnel to Changshu to negotiate with local people, intending to establish a branch here. It has contacted Gui Zhian, a local resident, and progress has been made. Preparations are currently underway. It is said that the branch is expected to be established in late next month.

Zhenjiang 95

Security Department Determines Construction Site: The Jiangsu Provincial Security Department has been established for a year, but the existing office space is inadequate. Previously, the department planned to construct new premises, but there was no suitable site. A request was submitted to the provincial government for the allocation of land for construction. The provincial government instructed that the former, disused Zhenjiang Prefecture and County City God Temple be allocated to the department for construction. Upon receiving the order, the department demarcated the area with stakes in accordance with the instructions and will commence reconstruction soon. A public notice was issued to inform everyone that any boundary disputes within the demarcated area must be submitted to the department for review within two weeks from today.

Director of Construction Department Inspects Sheng-Ju Road: Sun Hongzhe, Director of the Construction Department of Jiangsu Province, has recently been paying close attention to the construction of various highways. As the Sheng-Ju Road is an important route between Zhenjiang and Jurong, it is urgently necessary to expedite its construction to facilitate transportation between the two cities. To promote the progress of the road project, he personally traveled by car from the provincial capital to the Jurong area yesterday to inspect the road surface and provide guidance.

Fire at the Zhu Family Hamlet in the Western Suburbs: At around 11 p.m. the night before, a fire broke out at the home of Zhou Zhaolin, a citizen of the Zhu Family Hamlet in the western suburbs, due to embers left unattended in the kitchen. The accumulated firewood was ignited, and thick smoke quickly spread, engulfing the house. The family members were awakened from their sleep and rushed out without even getting dressed. Neighbors also came to draw water to extinguish the fire, but the fire was too fierce and difficult to control. It took an hour to extinguish the blaze. Nine households and twenty-five thatched houses were burned down. An elderly woman and four cattle were killed.

Rugao 96

Reasons for Wanted Notice for Shou Nengmo: The county government of this county holds regular meetings every Tuesday and Friday. December 12th last year was a Friday, and most of the committee members were away, so the meeting was postponed to the next day (the 13th). In the morning, the receiving and dispatch office sent an order from the Provincial Training Department regarding the National Salvation Fund to Shou. Shou then convened a meeting to discuss remitting the funds to the province. However, all the committee members considered the matter significant and required detailed discussion. The clerk then discovered many suspicious points in the order. Another committee member, Wang Taikui, telegraphed the Provincial Rectification Committee, which replied that there was no such matter. Shou left early in the morning of the 14th without even washing. Afterwards, the provincial party headquarters sent personnel to investigate and concluded that Shou was suspected of forging official documents. Repeated announcements were made in various newspapers in Shanghai and Hangzhou, summoning Shou to the party headquarters for questioning, but he failed to appear. Therefore, the provincial party headquarters sent a letter to the provincial government requesting the issuance of a warrant for his arrest in all counties.

Gaoyou 97

Fire at the Wu Family in the Eastern Suburbs: At around 10 p.m. last night, a fire broke out at the home of a farmer surnamed Wu in the eastern suburbs of this county due to carelessness with fire. Although the fire brigades of various shops arrived at the scene to extinguish the fire, the wind fueled the flames, rendering their efforts ineffective. It took four hours to extinguish the fire. More than ten houses and a cow were burned down. The loss is estimated to be several thousand yuan.

Educational News

Local News 99

City Education Bureau Prepares Social Studies and Natural Science Exhibition: The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau plans to hold an exhibition of achievements in social studies and natural science from elementary schools in the city in mid-May. This was previously reported. It is now reported that the Preparatory Committee convened its third meeting yesterday (the 13th) afternoon at the bureau. Attendees included Jiang Hongchao, Li Bojun, Chen Kunzhen, Zhao Lüqing, Gu Yinqian, Qian Xuanqing, Zhong Shike, Tang Jingxiu, Zhou Zhaonan, and others, totaling nine people. Jiang Hongchao presided over the meeting. The main agenda item was to appoint personnel for the five sections to carry out their work, and to draft a preparatory plan that has been approved by the bureau director. The plan is as follows: 1. The committee will be organized by nine members appointed by the Municipal Education Bureau to prepare all matters related to the exhibition. 2. The committee will be divided into five sections (General Affairs/Documentation, Accounting, Logistics, Registration/Exhibition, and Public Relations/Security). The preparatory committee members will be assigned to each section, and the bureau director may appoint additional personnel to assist when necessary. 3. The scope of collection of achievements for this committee is as follows: A. Schools: All municipal elementary schools in the city must submit their achievements for exhibition (unless there are special circumstances, which must be approved by the Education Bureau upon the school's request). 2. All registered private elementary schools in the city may also submit their achievements for exhibition. B. Achievements: 1. Student Work (a) Classwork (e.g., notes, problem answers, etc.). Each school should select and submit work samples from each grade, with the number of samples for each type accounting for one-fifth of the total number of students in that grade. (b) Projects: Schools should select and submit outstanding student projects, such as specimens, models, and charts. (c) Other student work: Schools may freely select and submit other types of student work. 3. Teaching Aids: (a) Original Teaching Aids: Schools should select and exhibit original teaching aids. (b) Reproduced Teaching Aids: Schools should select and exhibit reproduced teaching aids. (c) Purchased Teaching Aids: Schools should select and exhibit outstanding purchased teaching aids. 4. The procedure for exhibiting achievements of this committee is as follows: Schools' submissions must be accompanied by the registration forms and instructions prescribed by the committee, which must be completed and returned to the registration section five days before the meeting. The exhibition section will then allocate exhibition locations in advance. Schools must deliver their submissions to the exhibition site and display them in the designated locations on the day before the opening of the meeting. 5. The achievements of this committee will be exhibited by school. Each school will display its achievements by subject or in a combined display, depending on the content of the achievements. 6. The custody of the achievements of this committee will be the responsibility of the security section, and each school will also send personnel to safeguard its submissions during the exhibition hours each day. 7. The opening date of this committee is scheduled for May 15th, 16th, and 17th. 8. The opening location of this committee is scheduled for the Municipal Xicheng and Meixi Schools on Penglai Road in the Nanshi district. 9. The achievements of this committee will be reviewed by experts hired by the Education Bureau, who will select the best achievements for awards and compile a special booklet of outstanding achievements. 10. Each school must collect all of its achievements within one day after the closing of the meeting. 11. The preparatory committee for this committee will be dissolved after all schools have collected their achievements.

Experts Co-author "Marriage Guidance" 101

The book "Marriage Guidance," co-authored by seven experts including Hua Linsheng, former director of the Chinese Literature Department of Jinling Women's University, lawyer Qu Shao Yi, Liao Maoru, vice president of Guanghua University, Ai Wei, professor at Central University, Song Guobin, professor at Aurora University, Tang Qingzeng, professor at Great China University, and writer Xu Qingyu, has been published by the Qinfen Bookstore at No. 39 Xinmin Village, Malan Road, Shanghai. The book provides guidance on solving marriage problems for young men and women based on reason and explores topics such as ethics, law, education, economics, psychology, physiology, and aesthetics, which are greatly beneficial for young people. The book is beautifully printed and sells for 70 cents per copy, with a special price of 56 cents. It is available at the World, Kaiming, Wenming, and Taitung bookstores in this city, as well as at the Living Weekly magazine.

Foreign First Division Game

Lehua's First Victory 106

Defeated Portugal 4-3, Breaking the Losing Streak This Season: Since the Lehua Football Team separated from Jinan and returned to Huizhou, their strength has greatly declined and their reputation has plummeted. In various competitions of the Foreign Football Association this season, they have been defeated in every match without exception. Previously, they relied on the visit of the famous general Cao Guicheng to Shanghai to secure a draw, earning a single point and avoiding being shut out. Yesterday, they met Portugal at Shenyuan in the First Division Tournament. Fortunately, the Portuguese team was also in decline, and Lehua surprisingly won 4-3, winning two points and breaking the losing streak this season. When the good news came, it was unexpected. I record it here to inform the fans who were disappointed and did not attend. Referee: Li Silian.

(1) Lehua Achieved Unexpected Luck 107

Lehua's lineup yesterday was not better than before. Basic generals such as Zhou Xianyan and Chen Yutian were absent. Only the veterans Li Ning and Guan Xun'an supported the inside, and Zhou Shaowen fought on the outside. After ninety minutes of struggle, Zhou Shaowen contributed significantly and scored three goals alone. In the last ten minutes, the two teams were tied 3-3. At that time, Portugal attacked fiercely. Lehua was able to protect the goal thanks to the efforts of goalkeeper Huang Zonghua, and the inside defense and midfield also provided considerable assistance. A call to arms rallied the entire army to fight fiercely and advance with the ball into the goal. It is difficult to record the names on the merit list of who exactly scored the winning goal.

(2) Portugal Encountered Unexpected Circumstances 108

It is unbelievable that Portugal lost to Lehua, but it happened. It can be said to be an unexpected turn of events. Although, in terms of the strength of the players on the field, Portugal's strength is not much greater than Lehua's. Gu Stain, the famous central defender in Shanghai, had no one to replace him in goal. Inner defender Marcel and wingers Gertis and Lawson are the dangerous players for the Portuguese team. Of the three goals, one came from Fafan Que's feet, and the others came from the help of other players. After conceding two goals, they took the lead with three consecutive goals and seemed to be on track to secure victory. However, they conceded two more goals, ultimately leading to defeat. Losing the game is a common occurrence.

(3) Each Side Scored Two Goals in the First Half 109

Lehua kicked off, and the attack was not smooth. The enemy defended Li Jianbi, and the enemy repeatedly advanced and retreated. The Lehua forwards also advanced many times, but failed to score. After twenty minutes of stalemate, Lin Bingwen took the lead, went straight in from the border, and passed the ball in the middle. Zhou Shaowen greeted it with a kick and scored into the goal. More than two hundred spectators burst into laughter. In the laughter, the five Lehua players charged again. Zhou Shaowen did not disappoint and scored another goal. When the Portuguese team also launched a counterattack, Fafan Que took back a goal within six minutes. Two minutes later, Fafan Que dribbled the ball and explored the goal, but the inside was empty and only the goalkeeper was there. The ball was fast and urgent, and it was blocked but not far away. Fafan Que caught up and scored, making it a 2-2 tie. After that, there were storms once each, but no danger was created. Each side scored two goals in the first half.

(4) The Last Goal Determined the Victory 110

The teams changed sides and lined up again. The whistle blew and the battle resumed. The players were all agile, and everyone used their strength. Thirty minutes passed like a flash. Neither team made any progress. When the Portuguese player Fafan Que attacked the goal, he suddenly collided with the goalkeeper. The ball rolled into the goal on its own. The Portuguese team suddenly took a 3-2 lead. The Lehua forwards passed the ball to each other and advanced. Zhou Shaowen's kick became a 3-3 tie again. In the last ten minutes, the Lehua forwards fought each other in front of the enemy's goal. No one knew how they squeezed the ball in. With this goal, the victory was decided. Although the Portuguese team used all their strength, they could not get past goalkeeper Huang's last gate. As a result, Lehua won 4-3.

China Women Defeated England by a Wide Margin 116

32 to 10 ratio Women's United States 48 to 33 victory over the Federation Men's United States 62 to 19 victory over Korea The Shanghai International Basketball Championship held three games last night starting at 6:00 PM, all held at the China Basketball Hall. In the women's game, China defeated England 32-10, referee Shu Hong; the United States defeated the Federation 48-33, referee Shao Ji. In the men's game, the United States defeated Korea 62-19, referee Wang En.

China Crushed England 117

(Women)

The Chinese women's skills are indeed superior to those of England. Regardless of stealing, throwing, passing, and tactics, the entire team can always use clever means to defeat the enemy. Shao Jinying's skillfulness, Xi Jun's throws, Yang Ren's liveliness, and Gan Yunsheng's courage are truly unstoppable. The inner defense generals are also experienced and extremely rigorous. The tie with the Federation was due to bad luck. Yesterday, they showed their true colors against England. Xi Jun opened the scoring with a free throw, and Shao Jinying scored a direct hit, immediately taking a 3-0 lead. Berling scored a goal, and then Xi and Shao scored successively, taking a 3-0 lead. The British attacked with full force, but their throws were poor, with nine out of ten misses. In the first quarter, China scored ten points and England scored three points. In the second quarter, Yang Ren broke through the line and scored a goal. Shao Jinying scored twice with the help of her teammates. The enemy's momentum turned and they counterattacked strongly, but their throws were poor, with nine out of ten misses. China won the first half 18-13. In the third quarter, the Chinese team repeatedly changed players and their energy was abundant, scoring a total of eight points, while England did not score any points. The situation slowed down slightly in the last quarter, and each side scored. As a result, China defeated England 32-10.

Progress on the Sino-Turkish Treaty 120

The Turkish Chargé d'Affaires Visited Foreign Minister Wang Yesterday. It is understood that the commercial and friendship treaty between China and Turkey has been negotiated several times in Beijing by the Turkish Chargé d'Affaires, Fu Depei, and Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting. French Aviators Arrive in Shanghai 123

The long-distance flight from Paris to Tokyo may arrive at Hongqiao Airport today. French aviators Marnes and Belding are making a long-distance flight from Paris to Tokyo. They were originally scheduled to arrive in Shanghai yesterday. According to news from the French Consulate General, if the weather is good, the French aviators are expected to arrive today. Yesterday, the aviators stayed in Hong Kong temporarily due to poor weather in the south. The French aviators are flying a Farman aircraft with 230 horsepower. They departed from Paris on the 2nd of this month and hope to set a record for fast flight via Vietnam to Tokyo. Unexpectedly, the day after taking off from Paris, they encountered a storm and were forced to land in Aire-sur-l'Adour. The fuselage was damaged and delayed until the 9th before they could continue their flight to the Far East. They arrived in Hanoi four days later, and the flight time from Paris to Hanoi was 77 hours. Yesterday morning, they flew from Hanoi to Shanghai, stopping in Macau on the way before flying to Hong Kong. If the weather improves, the two aviators are expected to fly to Hongqiao Airport this afternoon.

Resolution of the Silk Industry Bonds 124

As a result of Chu Fucheng and others going to Beijing for the second time, the Silk Industry Group elected representatives, including Chu Fucheng, to petition for the issuance of bonds to rescue the silk industry. Representative Chu returned to Shanghai yesterday, and a reporter from the Daily News immediately visited him to inquire about the results of the trip. Representative Chu said that the case had been completely negotiated with the Ministry of Industry, the Ministry of Finance, and the Legislative Yuan. According to the original request of the silk industry, a total of 8 million yuan in bonds will be issued, of which 2 million yuan will be for improving sericulture, 2 million yuan will be for improving machinery, and 4 million yuan will be for rescuing the silk industry. However, before the Ministry of Industry begins to improve machinery, silk merchants can temporarily use this money to rescue the silk industry. As for the bond regulations, the Ministry of Finance has drafted them and submitted them to the Ministry of Industry for referral to the Legislative Yuan for approval and promulgation before they can be issued.

Tragedy on the Jiangshun Steamer 125

More than 90 gambling bandits killed and injured four cooks after the ship arrived at Huangshi Port. The ship arrived in Shanghai yesterday. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Jiangshun Steamer had a tragedy on its return trip from Hankou to Shanghai, with gamblers stabbing a cook to death at Huangshi Port. The ship arrived in Shanghai at about 5:00 PM yesterday and reported the details of the incident as follows:

The Reason for the Tragedy: It is found that there are gamblers, similar to discharged soldiers, who mingle on ships along the Yangtze River to swindle money. These gamblers are divided into two factions: the Hankou faction and the Huangshi Port faction. When the ship left Hankou on the 12th, there were eighty or ninety Hankou gamblers on board. They had long-standing animosity towards the Huangshi Port faction and intended to fight them with weapons. Therefore, they carried daggers, awls, and other weapons onto the ship and scattered themselves in the cabins. At 11:00 AM on the 13th, the ship arrived at Huangshi Port. These gamblers had already prepared on the ship, waiting for the gamblers from that location to board the ship before taking action. However, the Huangshi Port gamblers did not board the ship that day, so they could not fight even if they wanted to.

Assault and Injury of Four People: At that time, dinner was being prepared on the ship. Because these gamblers never buy tickets, they were not given dinner. Unexpectedly, the gamblers crowded to the entrance of the kitchen and asked the cook, Yan Er from Nanjing, for food. Yan Er and Wu Shengbao, Wu Laowu, and Luo Jinshan told them that the food was not yet cooked, but the gamblers insisted on taking it, and a verbal argument ensued. Unexpectedly, more than ten of the gamblers pulled out awls and daggers and stabbed Yan Er in the chest. Then, they twisted the knife with great force, and blood gushed out. Yan Er immediately fell to the ground and died. Wu Shengbao was also stabbed in the thigh and scrotum by a gambler and also fell to the ground. Wu Laowu and Luo Jinshan were stabbed in the hands. The ship's waiter saw this and quickly blew the whistle, and the bandits scattered and fled to the large cabins.

The Leader of the Bandits Tied Up a Criminal: The leader of the bandits, named Li Laowu, knew that he had caused a major disaster after the crime occurred. He dragged a bandit, a man in his forties wearing a blue cloth gown, to the entrance of the cabin and tied him up, saying that he was the perpetrator. However, the crew did not dare to punish the bandit, fearing that it would provoke a major incident.

Military Police in Jiujiang Arrested Bandits: At 4:00 PM, the ship arrived in Jiujiang. The ship immediately raised a distress flag and a doctor's flag and first sent Yu Qixiang, the ship's liaison officer, to shore in a sampan to report to the Garrison Headquarters and the Public Security Bureau. Soon, more than thirty police officers from the land and water Public Security Bureau arrived. They first prohibited passengers from disembarking in sampans, then ordered the Jiangshun to dock against the pontoon boat to inspect passengers landing ashore, and ordered the cooks to identify the perpetrators. Li Laowu, Tan Laowu, and seventeen others, including the tied-up criminal, were arrested on the spot and escorted to the Garrison Headquarters for interrogation. The other bandits had already taken off their uniforms and changed into plain clothes, so many escaped. Yan Da, the elder brother of the deceased cook, was also on the ship. The Jiujiang Public Security Bureau ordered him to temporarily collect and bury the body, and the seriously injured Wu Shengbao and others were sent to the Jiujiang Hospital. Xu Guisheng from the ship's relief room was left to guard the bay and await interrogation. At that time, the doctor of the British warship stationed in Xunyang also came to inspect and confirmed that Wu Shengbao's injuries were extremely serious. Yesterday afternoon, a telegram was received that Wu Shengbao had also died from his serious injuries.

The Crew Reported Back to Shanghai: After the ship arrested seventeen gamblers in Jiujiang, the other bandits, because they could not be identified, also disembarked in Haixun. On the same day, the Jiangshun first telegraphed Shanghai to report the incident and stated that there had been military police stationed on the ship, but they had recently been withdrawn by the Capital Garrison Command, which led to this unfortunate disaster. After the ship arrived in Shanghai yesterday, the shipowner had already asked Chief Li to telegraph Beijing to request the Garrison Command to reinstate the escorting military police to prevent similar tragedies from happening again.

Minutes of the Diplomatic Discussion Meeting 127

The 35th regular meeting of the Diplomatic Discussion Society was held at the Hong Kong Road Banking Association at 6:30 PM last night. Those present included Li Zhao, Liu Zhanen, Ye Huijun, Xia Weisong, Chen Shaoyou, Li Yingshi, Wu Zonglian, Gong Fengqiang, Xiao Jirong, Chu Huiseng, Xiang Weiqing, Li Qinghou, Shen Zhongjun, Zhang Xinglian, Huang Ruizheng, Shi Liangcai, Zhao Jinqing, Zhao Tiezhang, and more than twenty others. The agenda for the day was as follows: (A) Reporting Items (1) Committee Member Gong Fengqiang reported on the continued negotiation with Powell by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs regarding the establishment of an overseas news agency. (B) Discussion Items (1) Committee Member Ye Huijun proposed a suggestion to abolish consular jurisdiction. (2) Committee Member Chu Huiseng proposed to request the authorities to seriously negotiate with Japan regarding Japanese fishing boats arbitrarily entering our country's territorial waters to fish. (C) Temporary Motion: Second report on the establishment of an international news agency and newspaper, reporter Gong Fengqiang. Establishing an international news agency and newspaper in China now can be regarded as the most important thing for foreign affairs. However, with the national foundation just established and economic capabilities very weak, it is deeply difficult to establish such a great undertaking. However, it cannot be abandoned just because of fear of choking, and it cannot be shelved without doing anything. After spending half a year running around and consulting with various parties, the following methods have been obtained. Please decide whether they are appropriate: (1) The organization of this agency will be entirely commercial, with the government only providing one-time assistance at the time of establishment and no further subsidies thereafter. (2) The business of this agency is divided into three types: 1. Telegraph communication; 2. Daily newspaper; 3. Monthly magazine. (3) The headquarters of this agency will be located in Shanghai, with branches established in London, Paris, New York, Tokyo, Moscow, Berlin, Rome, and Geneva. Afterwards, it will be expanded to other locations. (4) The capital of this agency is set at one million yuan. Once 200,000 yuan of shares have been raised, the government will be requested to subsidize 200,000 yuan for the establishment. (5) The budget of this agency is the most difficult to determine. The following is a general report based on inquiries from various parties. Please study it further: 1. Daily Newspaper: The Shanghai headquarters will have a daily circulation of 50,000 copies, temporarily not counting profits. The English branch will have a circulation of 50,000 copies, the American branch 50,000 copies, the French branch 50,000 copies, the Soviet branch 50,000 copies, the Japanese branch 40,000 copies, the German branch 30,000 copies, the Italian branch 20,000 copies, and the Geneva branch 10,000 copies. The total circulation of the above eight locations is 300,000 copies. The annual newspaper fee for major newspapers in the United States, such as the New York Times, is US$32, while the Chicago Tribune is US$19.50 per year. The fees for other newspapers are generally similar. The fee for this agency should be cheaper when it is established, with an average of US$15. Advertising fees will also be extra cheap to attract customers. Each copy will have a net profit of US$1. The total profit of the eight locations will be US$300,000 per year. 2. The initial symptoms are red legs and unbearable pain. After bursting, there is a constant flow of pus and even more pain. This condition is especially common at the end of winter and the beginning of spring, and there is a lack of good remedies in the world, so patients suffer from it. (2) "Wishful Water for Chilblains" is used to treat unbroken chilblains to stop pain and itching immediately and eliminate redness and swelling. The price is extremely low. Discussion of the suggestion on how to abolish consular jurisdiction, proposed by Ye Huijun. Reason for the proposal: The abolition of consular jurisdiction by various countries in China is originally a diplomatic policy of the National Government and a work goal of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. In recent years, through the efforts of the authorities, many of these legal rights have been recovered. According to Foreign Minister Wang's report to reporters, there are a total of 25 countries that have treaty relations with China, of which 10 countries have no consular jurisdiction, 6 countries will also give up under certain circumstances, and the treaties of 3 countries have expired. Only 6 countries have treaties that have not expired, so the date of achieving the goal should not be far away. Recently, it has been reported that the authorities are conducting negotiations with the British and French envoys on this matter. Since this association is tasked with studying diplomatic strategies to contribute to the authorities, it seems that discussions and suggestions should be made as soon as possible for adoption. Please decide whether it is appropriate. Propose that the authorities seriously negotiate with Japan regarding Japanese fishing boats arbitrarily entering our country's territorial waters to fish, proposed by Committee Member Chu Huiseng. Reason for the proposal: It has been reported that Japanese fishing boats often enter our country's territorial waters to fish arbitrarily, and even hang our country's national flag and deliberately sink our country's fishing boats. It seems that such behavior not only infringes on our national sovereignty but also deprives our people of their livelihoods and must be stopped urgently. Since this association is tasked with paying attention to the suffering of the people, it seems that a request should be made to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for serious negotiations and demand compensation for sunk ships and other losses. Please decide whether it is appropriate.

Areas with Increased International Parcel Prices 129

The Directorate General of Posts will issue an order to all bureaus to handle it. The Directorate General of Posts of the Ministry of Communications has increased the price of gold, and the income from international postal fees calculated in gold pounds has had a significant impact. Recently, the Bureau has revised the list of international parcel fees for some countries, slightly increasing them to make up for the loss. The Bureau will issue an order to the 23 postal regions and 36 first-class post offices in the country to follow the revised international parcel list. The areas with revised price increases are: (1) Egypt, parcels shipped directly from Hong Kong; (2) Egyptian Sudan, shipped from Hong Kong; (3) Federated Malay States and South Seas Islands, shipped from Hong Kong. All shipments transported by British ships of the Blue Funnel Line will have their postage increased by one-third during the most recent period. After the order arrives at the postal regions, the price increase will be implemented.

Three Reports on the Burning of the "Daji" Steamer 130

The Exact Number of Dead Returning to Shanghai on the "Dade" Steamer: The "Daji" Steamer of the Dada Company, on the Shanghai-Yangzhou Route, Carelessly Encountered Disaster at Longjusha, Zhanghuang Port, Resulting in the Tragic Death of Over a Hundred People. Detailed accounts have been reported previously, but after the incident, the company dispatched the "Chuyuan" and "Chuting" steamers, which had not returned as of last night. The company's regular "Dade" steamer arrived in Shanghai at 7 p.m. Here is a further report on yesterday's situation:

The Heartbreak of Onlookers: Yesterday, family members of the "Daji" crew, having waited in vain for their return, knew their hopes were dashed. However, cut off from news, they could not be at peace. Therefore, they brought their families to the wharf to inquire and await the arrival of the "Dade" steamer. The "Dade" arrived at the port at 7 p.m., after they had been waiting expectantly for five or six hours. The chaotic scene and the news confirming the deaths of their loved ones drove some family members to near madness, wishing to die with them. Such tragic scenes defy description.

Registration of Names by Hometown Associations: The Tongru, Chonghai, and Qi Hometown Associations of the Nanshi district continued registering victims yesterday after beginning the day before. Many came to register. Some were single passengers who died and had no one to inquire for them, or whose fate was unknown. Their relatives in Shanghai registered on their behalf, so that the associations could handle the arrangements. The seven bodies previously recovered by a special patrol boat had also been photographed and displayed at the association's entrance. No one had claimed them as of yesterday. Crew Registration: In addition to those reported yesterday, more crew members registered yesterday, and it has been confirmed that Chief Officer Jiang Wu Yougen is dead, with his body kept at Zhanghuang Port awaiting transport. A list is provided below:

Engine Room Foreman Li Guoyuan (Substitute), Chief Officer Jiang Wu Yougen (Dead), Second Officer Tang Muzhao (Returned), Second Officer Wu Caigen (Dead), Third Officer Zheng Anfu (Did Not Return), Second Mate Wang Xingfa (Dead), Fourth Officer Qiu Changming (Substitute), Stoker A Si (Returned), Head Stoker Xin Shengfu (Dead), Stoker Mei Shao (Returned), Stoker Chen Ahong (Did Not Return), Assistant A Fu (Returned), Stoker Yongchang (Did Not Return), Assistant Fu Xue (Returned), Stoker A Feng (Did Not Return), Assistant Han Qing (Returned), Stoker A Xing (Substitute), Carpenter Wang Linsheng (Dead), Sailor Lin Dongsheng (Did Not Return), Bao Chu (Did Not Return), Lin Ayuan (Alive), Tang Aru (Did Not Return), Bai A Duo (Did Not Return), Tang Zongchang (Dead), Xin Shougen (Substitute, Did Not Return), Le Qinggen (Did Not Return), Shao Afu (Did Not Return), Feng Xingen (Did Not Return), Hong Shunlin (Substitute), Hong Agen (Did Not Return), He Shunlin (Did Not Return), Ming He (Did Not Return), Xin Ajin (Alive), Head Sailor Xiang Dongsheng (Alive), Sailor Wu Afang (Did Not Return), Oiler Shunzheng (Did Not Return), Sailor Li Lai (Substitute, Did Not Return), Oiler Yuan Xiangcai (Did Not Return), Kitchen A De, Zhuang Lian, A Qi, Liu Lazi, Yinsheng, Qingjiang, Ma Zi, A Si (One Substitute, All Alive), Li Asheng, Tian Jinrong, Fan Sheng's Brother-in-law, Yuan Aquan, Zhu Dacai, Newly Added One Person, Small Worker Liu Baohua, Xu Xiaoer, Zi Lu Dasun, Wu Lao Hu, Xiao Du, Zi Da Taozi, Xiao Wang Wu Yuanshen, Zi Wu Azi, Tang Baozhen, Xu Youlin, Hu Yougen, Hu Kou Xi, Xiao Sanzi, Da Xizi, Xiao Wang Wang Fuzi (All Did Not Return), Da Mazi (Dead), Ding Laosi, Lu Sanzong, Sun Changgui, Xu Shuangxin, Xu Xiaotaozi, Hu Youliang, Ge Xiaowuzi (All Did Not Return), Already Listed in Yesterday's Report, Not Repeated

"Dade" Returns to Shanghai: The Dada Company's "Dade" steamer was originally expected to return to Shanghai at 1 p.m. yesterday, but was delayed because it transported clothing and coffins from the Nantong Hometown Association to Tiansheng Port. It finally arrived in Shanghai at 7:30 p.m. According to those on board, a total of 150-160 bodies were recovered from Zhanghuang Port, Xin Port, Tiansheng Port, and other locations, and are now displayed at Zhanghuang Port awaiting photographs and coffins. The rescued survivors were eager to return to their hometowns and took separate ships from Zhanghuang Port to do so. None of the crew members took the "Dade" steamer back to Shanghai yesterday. Based on this, the total number of dead is estimated to be over 160. The refugees waiting for news, seeing that the "Dade" steamer did not bring their family members to Shanghai, dispersed, making the scene at the wharf even more desolate.

Confirmed Number of Dead: According to further reliable sources, 119 bodies were recovered from Zhanghuang Port, 11 from Tiansheng Port, and 22 from Xin Port, totaling 152 bodies. In addition, four bodies, including one girl, were burned on the ship and transported to Zhanghuang Port for burial. It is said that the burial arrangements are as follows: those who wish to use a shared coffin can have the company handle the burial; those who wish to provide their own coffins may do so. The purchasing agent of the steamer, Xu Jingzhai, provided coffins valued at 350 yuan, and a tea servant's family provided coffins valued at 150 yuan. It is reported that coffin shops have been bought out, with the Shaoning Hometown Association acting as an intermediary.

Company Meeting: The Dada Company is scheduled to hold a post-disaster meeting this afternoon to discuss the aftermath of the "Daji" accident.

Company Statement: Around 5 p.m. yesterday, reporters from various newspapers met with Mr. Jiang Decun of the company's board of directors. Mr. Jiang stated that the approximate details of the fire on the company's "Daji" steamer near Xinjiang on the 11th of this month have been reported in the newspapers. For more detailed information, the company must wait for the "Dade" steamer to return from Yangzhou. According to the regular schedule, the "Dade" steamer should have arrived in Shanghai at 2 p.m. today (yesterday), but it has not yet arrived, presumably because the ship is taking care of everything at the site of the accident, causing the delay (note: arrived at 7 p.m., see above). When the "Daji" steamer left Shanghai, it was carrying dozens of packages of sulfur, with wooden barriers to prevent passengers from entering to avoid danger. According to those who escaped from the ship and returned to Shanghai, more than 40 soldiers boarded the ship at Tiansheng Port and searched everywhere for suitable accommodation. Finding none, they discovered the sulfur storage area in the steerage cabin. Seeing that the area was spacious, they demanded that the ship's officers open the wooden barriers so they could settle inside. The officer refused, explaining the danger, but the soldiers were enraged and tore down the barriers, rushing in and occupying the space. The officer, seeing the situation, tried to persuade them not to smoke cigarettes, but the soldiers ignored him and soon gathered to gamble and smoke wildly. As a result, within four hours, a huge tragedy occurred, and we (the survivors) were unfortunately caught in the disaster. From this, the cause of the accident is clear. The company's iron barge was more than fifty miles away when it heard the alarm and immediately rushed to the scene to provide assistance. The Shanghai company also dispatched the "Chuting" and "Chuyuan" steamers to the area to recover bodies. Shortly after, we received a telegram from the "Chuyuan" and "Chuting" steamers stating that on the morning after the accident, they rescued more than 40 passengers on the beach. These passengers had been frozen unconscious after falling into the water and were swept to the shore, where they were spotted and rescued by fishermen. On the 12th, a total of 130 bodies were recovered, most of whom were crew members of the "Daji" steamer. The company immediately dispatched Mr. Zhu Xiaozhu, the purchasing agent of the "Dahe" steamer, along with the family members of the victims registered with the Tongchonghai Hometown Association, to rush to the area on the evening of the 13th aboard the "Dahe" steamer to purchase 140 coffins and photograph the deceased before burial, awaiting identification. The families of the victims have been requesting compensation from the company. However, the company has suffered an unexpected disaster and losses of hundreds of thousands of dollars, which is extremely unfortunate. Furthermore, according to the regulations of the Shipping Industry Association, accidents such as fires that occur on company ships operating at sea are not the fault of the ships. Therefore, requests for compensation from the families of the victims should be rejected. However, the company sees that the families of the victims are mostly poor and deserving of pity. Therefore, we have no dared to openly violate the resolutions of the Shipping Industry Association and have no choice but to entrust several directors of the board to the Jisheng Society to handle the compensation on our behalf. The Jisheng Society has agreed and will send staff to investigate the situation before formulating compensation regulations.
